48cdef enum Property: 

49 PROP_IS_UNIQUE = 1 << 0 

50 PROP_IS_CONTIGUOUS_C = 1 << 1 

51 PROP_IS_CONTIGUOUS_F = 1 << 2 

52 PROP_IS_CONTIGUOUS_ANY = 1 << 3 

53 PROP_IS_DENSE = 1 << 4 

54 PROP_OFFSET_BOUNDS = 1 << 5 

55 PROP_REQUIRED_SIZE_IN_BYTES = 1 << 6 

56 PROP_SHAPE = 1 << 7 

57 PROP_STRIDES = 1 << 8 

58 PROP_STRIDES_IN_BYTES = 1 << 9 

59 PROP_STRIDE_ORDER = 1 << 10 

60 PROP_VOLUME = 1 << 11 

61  

62  

63cdef struct BaseLayout: 

64 # A struct holding the shape and strides for the layout. 

65 # Use ``init_base_layout`` to initialize the layout, it will 

66 # set the ``shape`` and ``strides`` pointers to point to 

67 # ndim contigious integer arrays. 

68 # The ``shape`` pointer must not be NULL, the ``strides`` can be 

69 # set to NULL by the user to indicate C-contiguous layout. 

70 # Uses single _mem allocation to reduce overhead 

71 # (allocation and exceptions checks). 

72  

73 extents_strides_t _mem 

74 extent_t* shape 

75 stride_t* strides 

76 int ndim 

77  

78  

79@cython.final

81

83 cdef: 

84 BaseLayout base 

85

87 int itemsize 

88 stride_t slice_offset 

89  

90 # Lazy properties computed from the defining values. 

91 cdef: 

92 # Set to 0 to invalidate all properties, 

93 # whenever a defining value is changed 

94 property_mask_t _prop_mask 

95  

96 # C and Python properties 

97 property_mask_t _boolean_props 

98 int64_t _required_size_in_bytes 

99 stride_t _min_offset 

100 stride_t _max_offset 

101 int64_t _volume 

102  

103 # Python properties 

104 tuple _py_shape 

105 tuple _py_strides 

106 tuple _py_strides_in_bytes 

107 tuple _py_stride_order
